::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
# []{#sveltekit-on-vercel .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[SvelteKit on Vercel]{.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0} {#sveltekit-on-vercel .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2.5rem;--text-line-height:3.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.058125rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::::: {.[&_[data-geist-note]_p]:my-0 .[&_code_p]:my-0 .[&_code_p]:contents .[&_p]:leading-[1.6] .[&_ol]:p-0 .[&_ol]:pl-4 .[&_ol]:list-decimal .[&_ol]:ml-3.5 .[&_[class*='container']_p]:m-0}
SvelteKit is a frontend framework that enables you to build Svelte
applications with modern techniques, such as Server-Side Rendering,
automatic code splitting, and advanced routing.

You can deploy your SvelteKit projects to Vercel with zero
configuration, enabling you to use [Preview
Deployments](/docs/deployments/environments#preview-environment-pre-production){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}, [Web
Analytics](#web-analytics){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
zone="null"}, [Serverless
Functions](/docs/functions/serverless-functions){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}, and more.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#get-started-with-sveltekit-on-vercel .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Get started with SvelteKit on Vercel](#get-started-with-sveltekit-on-vercel){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#get-started-with-sveltekit-on-vercel .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

To get started with SvelteKit on Vercel:

- If you already have a project with SvelteKit, install [Vercel
  CLI](/docs/cli){.link_link__hbWKh .link_highlight__kJZF9 zone="same"}
  and run the `vercel`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
  command from your project\'s root directory
- Clone one of our SvelteKit example repos to your favorite git provider
  and deploy it on Vercel with the button below:

:::: styles_quickstart__eAz1g
[[]{.flex .w-11 .h-11 .mb-6}[Deploy our SvelteKit template, or view a
live
example.]{.quickstart_note__cP9uk}](/templates/svelte/sveltekit-boilerplate){.link_link__hbWKh
.quickstart_cardLink__MXwjP zone="vercel-site"}

Vercel deployments can [integrate with your git
provider](/docs/git){.link_link__hbWKh .link_highlight__kJZF9
zone="same"} to [generate preview
URLs](/docs/deployments/environments#preview-environment-pre-production){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_highlight__kJZF9 zone="same"} for each pull request you make to
your SvelteKit project.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#use-vercel-features-with-svelte .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Use Vercel features with Svelte](#use-vercel-features-with-svelte){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#use-vercel-features-with-svelte .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

When you create a new SvelteKit project with
`npm create svelte@latest`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn},
it installs `adapter-auto`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} by
default. This adapter detects that you\'re deploying on Vercel and
installs the `@sveltejs/adapter-vercel`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} plugin for you at build time.

We recommend installing the `@sveltejs/adapter-vercel`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} package yourself. Doing so will ensure version
stability, slightly speed up your CI process, and [allows you to
configure default deployment options for all routes in your
project](#configure-your-sveltekit-deployment){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="null"}.

The following instructions will guide you through adding the Vercel
adapter to your SvelteKit project.

1.  ::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
    ### []{#install-sveltekit's-vercel-adapter-plugin .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Install SvelteKit\'s Vercel adapter plugin](#install-sveltekit's-vercel-adapter-plugin){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#install-sveltekits-vercel-adapter-plugin .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:1.5rem;--text-line-height:2rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.029375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
    :::

    You can add [the Vercel
    adapter](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/adapter-vercel){.link_link__hbWKh
    .link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"} to
    your SvelteKit project by running the following command:

    ::::: {.relative .code-block_wrapper__t6FCO .code-block_custom__RWaXi .code-block_hideLineNumbers__52YKH geist-code-block=""}
    :::: tabs_tabsWrapper__szdGn

    pnpm
    yarn
    npm
    bun
    :::

    ![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNMi43NSAwLjVDMS43ODM1IDAuNSAxIDEuMjgzNSAxIDIuMjVWOS43NUMxIDEwLjcxNjUgMS43ODM1IDExLjUgMi43NSAxMS41SDMuNzVINC41VjEwSDMuNzVIMi43NUMyLjYxMTkzIDEwIDIuNSA5Ljg4ODA3IDIuNSA5Ljc1VjIuMjVDMi41IDIuMTExOTMgMi42MTE5MyAyIDIuNzUgMkg4LjI1QzguMzg4MDcgMiA4LjUgMi4xMTE5MyA4LjUgMi4yNVYzSDEwVjIuMjVDMTAgMS4yODM1IDkuMjE2NSAwLjUgOC4yNSAwLjVIMi43NVpNNy43NSA0LjVDNi43ODM1IDQuNSA2IDUuMjgzNSA2IDYuMjVWMTMuNzVDNiAxNC43MTY1IDYuNzgzNSAxNS41IDcuNzUgMTUuNUgxMy4yNUMxNC4yMTY1IDE1LjUgMTUgMTQuNzE2NSAxNSAxMy43NVY2LjI1QzE1IDUuMjgzNSAxNC4yMTY1IDQuNSAxMy4yNSA0LjVINy43NVpNNy41IDYuMjVDNy41IDYuMTExOTMgNy42MTE5MyA2IDcuNzUgNkgxMy4yNUMxMy4zODgxIDYgMTMuNSA2LjExMTkzIDEzLjUgNi4yNVYxMy43NUMxMy41IDEzLjg4ODEgMTMuMzg4MSAxNCAxMy4yNSAxNEg3Ljc1QzcuNjExOTMgMTQgNy41IDEzLjg4ODEgNy41IDEzLjc1VjYuMjVaIiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+)

2.  ::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
    ### []{#add-the-vercel-adapter-to-your-svelte-config .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Add the Vercel adapter to your Svelte config](#add-the-vercel-adapter-to-your-svelte-config){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#add-the-vercel-adapter-to-your-svelte-config .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:1.5rem;--text-line-height:2rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.029375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
    :::

    Add the Vercel adapter to your `svelte.config.js`{.code_code__TTx9V
    .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file, [which should be at the root of your
    project
    directory](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/configuration){.link_link__hbWKh
    .link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}.

    :::: {.note_note__W1ddN .v3-colors geist-note="" data-version="v1"}
    ::: {.note_content__kXdj4 style="gap:12px"}
    [![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOCAxNC41QzExLjU4OTkgMTQuNSAxNC41IDExLjU4OTkgMTQuNSA4QzE0LjUgNC40MTAxNSAxMS41ODk5IDEuNSA4IDEuNUM0LjQxMDE1IDEuNSAxLjUgNC40MTAxNSAxLjUgOEMxLjUgMTEuNTg5OSA0LjQxMDE1IDE0LjUgOCAxNC41Wk04IDE2QzEyLjQxODMgMTYgMTYgMTIuNDE4MyAxNiA4QzE2IDMuNTgxNzIgMTIuNDE4MyAwIDggMEMzLjU4MTcyIDAgMCAzLjU4MTcyIDAgOEMwIDEyLjQxODMgMy41ODE3MiAxNiA4IDE2Wk02LjI1IDdIN0g3Ljc0OTk5QzguMzAyMjcgNyA4Ljc0OTk5IDcuNDQ3NzIgOC43NDk5OSA4VjExLjVWMTIuMjVINy4yNDk5OVYxMS41VjguNUg3SDYuMjVWN1pNOCA2QzguNTUyMjkgNiA5IDUuNTUyMjggOSA1QzkgNC40NDc3MiA4LjU1MjI5IDQgOCA0QzcuNDQ3NzIgNCA3IDQuNDQ3NzIgNyA1QzcgNS41NTIyOCA3LjQ0NzcyIDYgOCA2WiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==)]{style="display:flex;height:16px"}
    You cannot use [TypeScript for your SvelteKit config
    file](https://github.com/sveltejs/kit/issues/2576){.link_link__hbWKh
    .link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}.
    :::
    ::::

    In your `svelte.config.js`{.code_code__TTx9V
    .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file, import `adapter`{.code_code__TTx9V
    .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} from
    `@sveltejs/adapter-vercel`{.code_code__TTx9V
    .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}, and add your preferred options. The
    following example shows the default configuration, which uses the
    Node.js runtime (which run on Vercel Serverless Functions).

    ::::::: {.relative .code-block_wrapper__t6FCO .code-block_hasFileName__ezlBD geist-code-block=""}
    :::::: code-block_header__t3NRd
    :::: code-block_fileName__HmSv1
    ::: {.code-block_iconWrapper__TuHFk aria-hidden="true"}

    ``` code-block_pre___OLfy
    import adapter from '@sveltejs/adapter-vercel';
     
    export default {
      kit: {
        adapter: adapter(),
      },
    };
    ```

## []{#configure-your-sveltekit-deployment .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Configure your SvelteKit deployment](#configure-your-sveltekit-deployment){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#configure-your-sveltekit-deployment .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

You can configure how your SvelteKit project gets deployed to Vercel at
the project-level and at the route-level.

Changes to the `config`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
object you define in `svelte.config.js`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} will affect the default settings for routes
across your whole project. To override this, you can export a
`config`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} object in any route
file.

The following is an example of a `svelte.config.js`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file that will deploy using server-side
rendering in Vercel\'s Node.js 18.x serverless runtime:

::::::: {.relative .code-block_wrapper__t6FCO .code-block_hasFileName__ezlBD geist-code-block=""}
:::::: code-block_header__t3NRd
:::: code-block_fileName__HmSv1
::: {.code-block_iconWrapper__TuHFk aria-hidden="true"}

::::::

``` code-block_pre___OLfy
import adapter from '@sveltejs/adapter-vercel';
 
/** @type {import('@sveltejs/kit').Config} */
const config = {
  kit: {
    adapter: adapter({
      runtime: 'nodejs18.x',
    }),
  },
};
 
export default config;
```
:::::::

You can also configure how individual routes deploy by exporting a
`config`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} object. The
following is an example of a route that will deploy on Vercel\'s Edge
runtime:

SvelteKit\'s docs have [a comprehensive list of all config options
available to
you](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/adapter-vercel#deployment-configuration){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}. This
section will cover a select few options which may be easier to use with
more context.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
#### []{#split .linked-heading_target__xscdv}[`split`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}](#split){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#split .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:1.25rem;--text-line-height:1.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.020625rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

By default, your SvelteKit routes get bundled into one Function when you
deploy your project to Vercel. This configuration typically reduces how
often your users encounter [cold
starts[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9IndpZHRoOjE0cHg7aGVpZ2h0OjE0cHg7Y29sb3I6Y3VycmVudENvbG9yIiB2aWV3Ym94PSIwIDAgMTYgMTYiIHdpZHRoPSIxNiI+PHBhdGggZmlsbC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBjbGlwLXJ1bGU9ImV2ZW5vZGQiIGQ9Ik0wIDFIMC43NUg1QzYuMjI2NyAxIDcuMzE1ODMgMS41ODkwMSA4IDIuNDk5NjNDOC42ODQxNyAxLjU4OTAxIDkuNzczMyAxIDExIDFIMTUuMjVIMTZWMS43NVYxM1YxMy43NUgxNS4yNUgxMC43NDI2QzEwLjE0NTkgMTMuNzUgOS41NzM2MSAxMy45ODcxIDkuMTUxNjUgMTQuNDA5TDguNTMwMzMgMTUuMDMwM0g3LjQ2OTY3TDYuODQ4MzUgMTQuNDA5QzYuNDI2MzkgMTMuOTg3MSA1Ljg1NDEgMTMuNzUgNS4yNTczNiAxMy43NUgwLjc1SDBWMTNWMS43NVYxWk03LjI1IDQuNzVDNy4yNSAzLjUwNzM2IDYuMjQyNjQgMi41IDUgMi41SDEuNVYxMi4yNUg1LjI1NzM2QzUuOTY3ODYgMTIuMjUgNi42NTc1OCAxMi40NTE2IDcuMjUgMTIuODIzMlY0Ljc1Wk04Ljc1IDEyLjgyMzJWNC43NUM4Ljc1IDMuNTA3MzYgOS43NTczNiAyLjUgMTEgMi41SDE0LjVWMTIuMjVIMTAuNzQyNkMxMC4wMzIxIDEyLjI1IDkuMzQyNDIgMTIuNDUxNiA4Ljc1IDEyLjgyMzJaIiBmaWxsPSJjdXJyZW50Q29sb3IiIC8+PC9zdmc+)]{.ml-1}](/docs/infrastructure/compute#cold-and-hot-boots){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_highlight__kJZF9 state="closed" zone="same"}.

[In most cases, there is no need to modify this
option]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}.

Setting `split: true`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} in your
Svelte config will cause your SvelteKit project\'s routes to get split
into separate Vercel Functions.

Splitting your Functions is not typically better than bundling them. You
may want to consider setting `split: true`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} if you\'re experiencing either of the following
issues:

- [You have exceeded the Function size limit for the runtime you\'re
  using]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}. Batching too many routes into a
  single Function could cause you to exceed Function size limits for
  your Vercel account. See our [Function size
  limits](/docs/limits#serverless-function-size){.link_link__hbWKh
  .link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} to learn more.
- [Your app is experiencing abnormally long cold start
  times]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}. Batching Serverless Functions into
  one Function will reduce how often users experience cold starts. It
  can also increase the latency they experience when a cold start is
  required, since larger functions tend to require more resources. This
  can result in slower responses to user requests that occur after your
  Function spins down.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
#### []{#regions .linked-heading_target__xscdv}[`regions`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}](#regions){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#regions .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:1.25rem;--text-line-height:1.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.020625rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Choosing a region allows you to reduce latency for requests to
functions. If you choose a Function region geographically near
dependencies, or nearest to your visitor, you can reduce your
Functions\' latency.

By default, your Vercel Functions will be deployed in *Washington, D.C.,
USA*, or `iad1`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}. Adding a
region ID to the `regions`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
array will deploy your Serverless Functions there. [See our Serverless
Function regions docs to learn how to override this
settings](/docs/functions/serverless-functions/regions#select-a-default-serverless-region){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#streaming .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Streaming](#streaming){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#streaming .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Vercel supports streaming API responses over time with SvelteKit,
allowing you to render parts of the UI early, then render the rest as
data becomes available. Doing so lets users interact with your app
before the full page loads, improving their perception of your app\'s
speed. Here\'s how it works:

- SvelteKit enables you to use a `+page.server.ts`{.code_code__TTx9V
  .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file to fetch data on the server, which you
  can access from a `+page.svelte`{.code_code__TTx9V
  .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file located in the same folder
- You fetch data in a [`load`{.code_code__TTx9V
  .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/load){.link_link__hbWKh
  .link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}
  function defined in `+page.server.ts`{.code_code__TTx9V
  .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}. This function returns an object
  - Top-level properties that return a promise will resolve before the
    page renders
  - Nested properties that return a promise [will
    stream](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/load#streaming-with-promises){.link_link__hbWKh
    .link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}

The following example demonstrates a `load`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} function that will stream its response to the
client. To simulate delayed data returned from a promise, it uses a
`sleep`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} method.

::::::::: {.relative .code-block_wrapper__t6FCO .code-block_hasFileName__ezlBD geist-code-block=""}

``` code-block_pre___OLfy
function sleep(value: any, ms: number) {
  // Use this sleep function to simulate
  // a delayed API response.
  return new Promise((fulfill) => {
    setTimeout(() => {
      fulfill(value);
    }, ms);
  });
}
export function load(event): PageServerLoad<any> {
  // Get some location data about the visitor
  const ip = event.getClientAddress();
  const city = decodeURIComponent(
    event.request.headers.get('x-vercel-ip-city') ?? 'unknown',
  );
  return {
    topLevelExample: sleep({ data: "This won't be streamed" }, 2000)
    // Stream the location data to the client
    locationData: {
      details: sleep({ ip, city }, 1000),
    },
  };
}
```

`+page.svelte`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file in the
same directory:

``` code-block_pre___OLfy
<script lang="ts">
  import type { PageData } from './$types'
  export let data: PageData;
</script>
 
<h1><span>Hello!</span></h1>
 
<div class="info">
  {#await data.locationData.details}
    <p>streaming delayed data from the server...</p>
  {:then details}
    <div>
      <p>City is {details.city}</p>
      <p>And IP is: {details.ip} </p>
    </div>
  {/await}
</div>
```
:::::::::

[To summarize, Streaming with SvelteKit on
Vercel:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Enables you to stream UI elements as data loads
- Supports streaming through Vercel Functions
- Improves perceived speed of your app

[Learn more about Streaming on
Vercel](/docs/functions/streaming-functions){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

## []{#server-side-rendering .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Server-Side Rendering](#server-side-rendering){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#server-side-rendering .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Server-Side Rendering (SSR) allows you to render pages dynamically on
the server. This is useful for pages where the rendered data needs to be
unique on every request. For example, verifying authentication or
checking the geolocation of an incoming request.

Vercel offers SSR that scales down resource consumption when traffic is
low, and scales up with traffic surges. This protects your site from
accruing costs during periods of no traffic or losing business during
high-traffic periods.

SvelteKit projects are server-side rendered by default. You can
configure individual routes to prerender with the
`prerender`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} page option, or
use the same option in your app\'s root `+layout.js`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} or `+layout.server.js`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file to make all your routes prerendered by
default.

[While server-side rendered SvelteKit apps do support middleware,
SvelteKit does not support URL rewrites from
middleware]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}.

[See the SvelteKit docs on prerendering to learn
more](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/page-options#prerender){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}.

[To summarize, SSR with SvelteKit on Vercel:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Scales to zero when not in use
- Scales automatically with traffic increases
- Has zero-configuration support for [`Cache-Control`{.code_code__TTx9V
  .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
  headers](/docs/edge-network/caching){.link_link__hbWKh
  .link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}, including
  `stale-while-revalidate`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}

[Learn more about
SSR](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/page-options#ssr){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#environment-variables .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Environment variables](#environment-variables){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#environment-variables .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Vercel provides a set of System Environment Variables that our platform
automatically populates. For example, the
`VERCEL_GIT_PROVIDER`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
variable exposes the Git provider that triggered your project\'s
deployment on Vercel.

These environment variables will be available to your project
automatically, and you can enable or disable them in your project
settings on Vercel. [See our Environment Variables docs to learn
how](/docs/environment-variables/system-environment-variables){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
### []{#use-vercel-environment-variables-with-sveltekit .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Use Vercel environment variables with SvelteKit](#use-vercel-environment-variables-with-sveltekit){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#use-vercel-environment-variables-with-sveltekit .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:1.5rem;--text-line-height:2rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.029375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

SvelteKit allows you to import environment variables, but separates them
into different modules based on whether they\'re dynamic or static, and
whether they\'re private or public. For example, the
`'$env/static/private'`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
module exposes environment variables that [don\'t
change]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}, and that you [should not share
publicly]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}.

[System Environment
Variables](/docs/environment-variables/system-environment-variables){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} are private and you should never expose
them to the frontend client. This means you can only import them from
`'$env/static/private'`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} or
`'$env/dynamic/private'`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}.

The example below exposes `VERCEL_COMMIT_REF`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn}, a variable that exposes the name of the branch
associated with your project\'s deployment, to [a
`load`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
function](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/load){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"} for a
Svelte layout:

``` code-block_pre___OLfy
import { LayoutServerLoad } from './types';
import { VERCEL_COMMIT_REF } from '$env/static/private';
 
type DeploymentInfo = {
  deploymentGitBranch: string;
};
 
export function load(): LayoutServerLoad<DeploymentInfo> {
  return {
    deploymentGitBranch: 'Test',
  };
}
```
:::::::::

You could reference that variable in [a corresponding
layout](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/load#layout-data){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"} as shown
below:

[To summarize, the benefits of using Environment Variables with
SvelteKit on Vercel include:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Access to vercel deployment information, dynamically or statically,
  with our preconfigured System Environment Variables
- Access to automatically-configured environment variables provided by
  [integrations for your preferred
  services](/docs/environment-variables#integration-environment-variables){.link_link__hbWKh
  .link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}
- Searching and filtering environment variables by name and environment
  in Vercel\'s dashboard

[Learn more about Environment
Variables](/docs/environment-variables){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}

## []{#incremental-static-regeneration-isr .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Incremental Static Regeneration (ISR)](#incremental-static-regeneration-isr){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#incremental-static-regeneration-isr .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Incremental Static Regeneration allows you to create or update content
without redeploying your site. When you deploy a route with ISR, Vercel
caches the page to serve it to visitors statically, and rebuilds it on a
time interval of your choice. ISR has three main benefits for
developers: better performance, improved security, and faster build
times.

[See our ISR docs to learn
more](/docs/incremental-static-regeneration){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

To deploy a SvelteKit route with ISR:

- Export a `config`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} object
  with an `isr`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} property. Its
  value will be the number of seconds to wait before revalidating
- To enable on-demand revalidation, add the
  `bypassToken`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} property to
  the `config`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} object. Its
  value gets checked when `GET`{.code_code__TTx9V
  .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} or `HEAD`{.code_code__TTx9V
  .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} requests get sent to the route. If the
  request has a `x-prerender-revalidate`{.code_code__TTx9V
  .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} header with the same value as
  `bypassToken`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}, the cache
  will be revalidated immediately

The following example demonstrates a SvelteKit route that Vercel will
deploy with ISR, revalidating the page every 60 seconds, with on-demand
revalidation enabled:

SvelteKit](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/adapter-vercel#incremental-static-regeneration){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}.

[To summarize, the benefits of using ISR with SvelteKit on Vercel
include:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Better performance with our global [Edge
  Network](/docs/edge-network){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
  zone="same"}
- Zero-downtime rollouts to previously statically generated pages
- Framework-aware infrastructure enables global content updates in 300ms
- Generated pages are both cached and persisted to durable storage

[Learn more about
ISR](/docs/incremental-static-regeneration){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}

## []{#skew-protection .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Skew Protection](#skew-protection){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#skew-protection .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

New project deployments can lead to [version
skew]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}. This can happen when your users are
using your app and a new version gets deployed. Their deployment version
requests assets from an older version. And those assets from the
previous version got replaced. This can cause errors when those active
users navigate or interact with your project.

SvelteKit has a skew protection solution. When it detects version skew,
it triggers a hard reload of a page to sync to the latest version. This
does mean the client-side state gets lost. With Vercel skew protection,
client requests get routed to their original deployment. No client-side
state gets lost. To enable it, visit the Advanced section of your
project settings on Vercel.

[Learn more about skew protection with
SvelteKit](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/adapter-vercel#skew-protection){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"}.

[To summarize, the benefits of using ISR with SvelteKit on Vercel
include:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Mitigates the risk of your active users encountering version skew
- Avoids hard reloads for current active users on your project

[Learn more about skew protection on
Vercel](/docs/skew-protection){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
zone="same"}.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#image-optimization .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Image Optimization](#image-optimization){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#image-optimization .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

[Image Optimization](/docs/image-optimization){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} helps you achieve faster page loads by
reducing the size of images and using modern image formats.

When deploying to Vercel, you can optimize your images on demand,
keeping your build times fast while improving your page load performance
and [Core Web
Vitals](/docs/speed-insights/metrics#core-web-vitals-explained){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

To use Image Optimization with SvelteKit on Vercel, use the
[`@sveltejs/adapter-vercel`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn}](#use-vercel-features-with-svelte){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="null"} within your
`svelte.config.ts`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file.

``` code-block_pre___OLfy
import adapter from '@sveltejs/adapter-vercel';
 
export default {
  kit: {
    adapter({
      images: {
        sizes: [640, 828, 1200, 1920, 3840],
        formats: ['image/avif', 'image/webp'],
        minimumCacheTTL: 300,
        domains: ['example-app.vercel.app'],
      }
    })
  }
};
```
:::::::::

This allows you to specify [configuration
options](https://vercel.com/docs/build-output-api/v3/configuration#images){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"} for
Vercel\'s native image optimization API.

To use image optimization with SvelteKit, you have to construct your own
`srcset`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} URLs. You can create
a library function that will optimize `srcset`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} URLs in production for you like this:

::::::::: {.relative .code-block_wrapper__t6FCO .code-block_hasFileName__ezlBD geist-code-block=""}

::::::::

``` code-block_pre___OLfy
import { dev } from '$app/environment';
 
export function optimize(src: string, widths = [640, 960, 1280], quality = 90) {
  if (dev) return src;
 
  return widths
    .slice()
    .sort((a, b) => a - b)
    .map((width, i) => {
      const url = `/_vercel/image?url=${encodeURIComponent(src)}&w=${width}&q=${quality}`;
      const descriptor = i < widths.length - 1 ? ` ${width}w` : '';
      return url + descriptor;
    })
    .join(', ');
}
```
:::::::::

Use an `img`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} or any other
image component with an optimized `srcset`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} generated by the `optimize`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} function:

::::::::: {.relative .code-block_wrapper__t6FCO .code-block_hasFileName__ezlBD geist-code-block=""}

``` code-block_pre___OLfy
<script lang="ts">
  import { optimize } from '$lib/image';
  import type { Photo } from '$lib/types';
 
  export let photo: Photo;
</script>
 
<img
  class="absolute left-0 top-0 w-full h-full"
  srcset={optimize(photo.url)}
  alt={photo.description}
/>
```
:::::::::

[To summarize, using Image Optimization with SvelteKit on
Vercel:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Configure image optimization with
  `@sveltejs/adapter-vercel`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
- Optimize for production with a function that constructs optimized
  `srcset`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} for your images
- Helps your team ensure great performance by default
- Keeps your builds fast by optimizing images on-demand

[Learn more about Image
Optimization](/docs/image-optimization){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}

## []{#web-analytics .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Web Analytics](#web-analytics){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#web-analytics .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Vercel\'s Web Analytics features enable you to visualize and monitor
your application\'s performance over time. The
[Analytics]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5} tab in your project\'s dashboard
offers detailed insights into your website\'s visitors, with metrics
like top pages, top referrers, and user demographics.

To use Web Analytics, navigate to the Analytics tab of your project
dashboard on Vercel and select [Enable]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5} in
the modal that appears.

To track visitors and page views, we recommend first installing our
`@vercel/analytics`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} package
by running the terminal command below in the root directory of your
SvelteKit project:

.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file, add the following
`<script>`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}:

With the above script added to your project, you\'ll be able to view
detailed user insights in your dashboard on Vercel under the Analytics
tab. [See our docs to learn more about the user metrics you can track
with Vercel\'s Web Analytics](/docs/analytics){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

[Your project must be deployed on Vercel to take advantage of the Web
Analytics feature]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}. Work on making this
feature more broadly available is in progress.

[To summarize, using Web Analytics with SvelteKit on
Vercel:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Enables you to track traffic and see your top-performing pages
- Offers you detailed breakdowns of visitor demographics, including
  their OS, browser, geolocation, and more

[Learn more about Web Analytics](/docs/analytics){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}

## []{#speed-insights .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Speed Insights](#speed-insights){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#speed-insights .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

You can see data about your project\'s [Core Web
Vitals](/docs/speed-insights#core-web-vitals-explained){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} performance in your dashboard on Vercel.
Doing so will allow you to track your web application\'s loading speed,
responsiveness, and visual stability so you can improve the user
experience.

[See our Speed Insights docs to learn
more](/docs/speed-insights){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
zone="same"}.

[To summarize, using Speed Insights with SvelteKit on
Vercel:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Enables you to track traffic performance metrics, such as [First
  Contentful
  Paint](/docs/speed-insights#first-contentful-paint-fcp){.link_link__hbWKh
  .link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}, or [First Input
  Delay](/docs/speed-insights#first-input-delay-fid){.link_link__hbWKh
  .link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}
- Enables you to view performance metrics by page name and URL for more
  granular analysis
- Shows you [a score for your app\'s
  performance](/docs/speed-insights#how-the-scores-are-determined){.link_link__hbWKh
  .link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} on each recorded metric, which you can
  use to track improvements or regressions

[Learn more about Speed
Insights](/docs/speed-insights){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
zone="same"}

:::

[Draft Mode](/docs/draft-mode){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
zone="same"} enables you to view draft content from your [Headless
CMS](/docs/solutions/cms){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
zone="same"} immediately, while still statically generating pages in
production.

To use a SvelteKit route in Draft Mode, you must:

1.  Export a `config`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} object
    [that enables Incremental Static
    Regeneration](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/adapter-vercel#incremental-static-regeneration){.link_link__hbWKh
    .link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"} from
    the route\'s `+page.server`{.code_code__TTx9V
    .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} file:

``` code-block_pre___OLfy
import { BYPASS_TOKEN } from '$env/static/private';
 
export const config = {
  isr: {
    // Random token that can be provided to bypass the cached version of the page with a __prerender_bypass=<token> cookie. Allows rendering content at request time for this route.
    bypassToken: BYPASS_TOKEN,
 
    // Expiration time (in seconds) before the cached asset will be re-generated by invoking the Serverless Function.
    // Setting the value to `false` means it will never expire.
    expiration: 60,
  },
};
```
:::::::::

2.  Send a `__prerender_bypass`{.code_code__TTx9V
    .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} cookie with the same value as
    `bypassToken`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn} in your
    config.

To render the draft content, SvelteKit will check for
`__prerender_bypass`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}. If its
value matches the value of `bypassToken`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn}, it will render content fetched at request time
rather than prebuilt content.

:::: {.note_note__W1ddN .v3-colors geist-note="" data-version="v1"}
::: {.note_content__kXdj4 style="gap:12px"}
[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOCAxNC41QzExLjU4OTkgMTQuNSAxNC41IDExLjU4OTkgMTQuNSA4QzE0LjUgNC40MTAxNSAxMS41ODk5IDEuNSA4IDEuNUM0LjQxMDE1IDEuNSAxLjUgNC40MTAxNSAxLjUgOEMxLjUgMTEuNTg5OSA0LjQxMDE1IDE0LjUgOCAxNC41Wk04IDE2QzEyLjQxODMgMTYgMTYgMTIuNDE4MyAxNiA4QzE2IDMuNTgxNzIgMTIuNDE4MyAwIDggMEMzLjU4MTcyIDAgMCAzLjU4MTcyIDAgOEMwIDEyLjQxODMgMy41ODE3MiAxNiA4IDE2Wk02LjI1IDdIN0g3Ljc0OTk5QzguMzAyMjcgNyA4Ljc0OTk5IDcuNDQ3NzIgOC43NDk5OSA4VjExLjVWMTIuMjVINy4yNDk5OVYxMS41VjguNUg3SDYuMjVWN1pNOCA2QzguNTUyMjkgNiA5IDUuNTUyMjggOSA1QzkgNC40NDc3MiA4LjU1MjI5IDQgOCA0QzcuNDQ3NzIgNCA3IDQuNDQ3NzIgNyA1QzcgNS41NTIyOCA3LjQ0NzcyIDYgOCA2WiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==)]{style="display:flex;height:16px"}

We recommend using a cryptographically secure random number generator at
build time as your `bypassToken`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} value. If a malicious actor guesses your
`bypassToken`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}, they can view
your pages in Draft Mode.
:::
::::

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
### []{#draft-mode-security .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Draft Mode security](#draft-mode-security){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#draft-mode-security .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:1.5rem;--text-line-height:2rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.029375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Deployments on Vercel automatically secure Draft Mode behind the same
authentication used for Preview Comments. In order to enable or disable
Draft Mode, the viewer must be logged in as a member of the
[Team](/docs/teams-and-accounts){.link_link__hbWKh .link_blend__JjXMT
zone="same"}. Once enabled, Vercel\'s Edge Network will bypass the ISR
cache automatically and invoke the underlying [Serverless
Function](/docs/functions/serverless-functions){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
### []{#enabling-draft-mode-in-preview-deployments .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Enabling Draft Mode in Preview Deployments](#enabling-draft-mode-in-preview-deployments){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#enabling-draft-mode-in-preview-deployments .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:1.5rem;--text-line-height:2rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.029375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

You and your team members can toggle Draft Mode in the Vercel Toolbar in
[production](/docs/vercel-toolbar/in-production-and-localhost/add-to-production){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"},
[localhost](/docs/vercel-toolbar/in-production-and-localhost/add-to-localhost){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}, and [Preview
Deployments](/docs/deployments/environments#preview-environment-pre-production#comments){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}. When you do so, the toolbar will become
purple to indicate Draft Mode is active.

style="margin-block:40px">

<figcaption>The Vercel toolbar when Draft Mode is enabled.</figcaption>

Users outside your Vercel team cannot toggle Draft Mode.

[To summarize, the benefits of using Draft Mode with SvelteKit on Vercel
include:]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}

- Easily server-render previews of static pages
- Adds security measures to prevent malicious usage
- Integrates with any headless provider of your choice
- You can enable and disable Draft Mode in [the comments
  toolbar](/docs/comments/how-comments-work){.link_link__hbWKh
  .link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} on Preview Deployments

[Learn more about Draft Mode](/docs/draft-mode){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"}

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#edge-middleware .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Edge Middleware](#edge-middleware){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#edge-middleware .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Edge Middleware is useful for modifying responses before they\'re sent
to a user. [We recommend [using SvelteKit\'s server
hooks](https://kit.svelte.dev/docs/hooks){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT rel="noopener" target="_blank" zone="null"} to modify
responses]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}. Due to SvelteKit\'s client-side
rendering, you cannot use Vercel\'s Edge Middleware with SvelteKit.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
## []{#rewrites .linked-heading_target__xscdv .linked-heading_offsetTop__uAoyO}[Rewrites](#rewrites){.linked-heading_title__mCMLh .[&>p]:m-0}[![](data:image/svg+xml;base64,PHN2ZyBjbGFzcz0idGV4dC1bMC42ZW1dIiBkYXRhLXRlc3RpZD0iZ2Vpc3QtaWNvbiIgaGVpZ2h0PSIxNiIgc3Ryb2tlLWxpbmVqb2luPSJyb3VuZCIgc3R5bGU9ImNvbG9yOmN1cnJlbnRDb2xvciIgdmlld2JveD0iMCAwIDE2IDE2IiB3aWR0aD0iMTYiPjxwYXRoIGZpbGwtcnVsZT0iZXZlbm9kZCIgY2xpcC1ydWxlPSJldmVub2RkIiBkPSJNOC40Njk2OCAxLjQ2OTY4QzEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgLTAuMjAzOTIzIDE0LjUzMDMgMS40Njk2OEMxNi4yMDM5IDMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1Njc0IDE0LjUzMDMgNy41MzAzNEwxMi4wMzAzIDEwLjAzMDNMMTAuOTY5NyA4Ljk2OTY4TDEzLjQ2OTcgNi40Njk2OEMxNC41NTc1IDUuMzgxODYgMTQuNTU3NSAzLjYxODE2IDEzLjQ2OTcgMi41MzAzNEMxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAxLjQ0MjUyIDkuNTMwMzQgMi41MzAzNEw3LjAzMDM0IDUuMDMwMzRMNS45Njk2OCAzLjk2OTY4TDguNDY5NjggMS40Njk2OFpNMTEuNTMwMyA1LjUzMDM0TDUuNTMwMzQgMTEuNTMwM0w0LjQ2OTY4IDEwLjQ2OTdMMTAuNDY5NyA0LjQ2OTY4TDExLjUzMDMgNS41MzAzNFpNMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzQzMuMTQzMjkgMTYuMjAzOSA1Ljg1NjczIDE2LjIwNCA3LjUzMDM0IDE0LjUzMDNMMTAuMDMwMyAxMi4wMzAzTDguOTY5NjggMTAuOTY5N0w2LjQ2OTY4IDEzLjQ2OTdDNS4zODE4NiAxNC41NTc1IDMuNjE4MTYgMTQuNTU3NSAyLjUzMDM0IDEzLjQ2OTdDMS40NDI1MiAxMi4zODE5IDEuNDQyNTIgMTAuNjE4MiAyLjUzMDM0IDkuNTMwMzRMNS4wMzAzNCA3LjAzMDM0TDMuOTY5NjggNS45Njk2OEwxLjQ2OTY4IDguNDY5NjhDLTAuMjAzOTIzIDEwLjE0MzMgLTAuMjAzOTI1IDEyLjg1NjcgMS40Njk2OCAxNC41MzAzWiIgZmlsbD0iY3VycmVudENvbG9yIiAvPjwvc3ZnPg==){.text-[0.6em]}]{.linked-heading_permalink__pJ_q_} {#rewrites .text_wrapper__i87JK .linked-heading_header__YpMmf .headings_heading__DRlSP data-version="v1" style="--text-color:var(--ds-gray-1000);--text-size:2rem;--text-line-height:2.5rem;--text-letter-spacing:-0.049375rem;--text-weight:600" components-heading="true"}
:::

Adding a [`vercel.json`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn}](/docs/project-configuration){.link_link__hbWKh
.link_blend__JjXMT zone="same"} file to the root directory of your
project enables you to rewrite your app\'s routes.

[We do not recommend using `vercel.json`{.code_code__TTx9V
.code_inlineCode__DZHMn} rewrites with
SvelteKit]{.strong_docsString__rhKq5}.

Rewrites from `vercel.json`{.code_code__TTx9V .code_inlineCode__DZHMn}
only apply to the Vercel proxy. At runtime, SvelteKit doesn\'t have
access to the rewritten URL, which means it has no way of rendering the
intended rewritten route.

::: linked-heading_container__iwdxj
